TUR_remove_current_sultan = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_abdulhamid_ii
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_abdulhamid_ii
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = HJZ_hussein_bin_ali_caliph
		}
		remove_ideas = HJZ_hussein_bin_ali_caliph
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_vi
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_vi
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_abdulmecid_ii
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_abdulmecid_ii
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_ahmed_nihad
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_ahmed_nihad
	}
}
TUR_increase_literacy = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_1
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_2
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_3
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_4
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_5
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_6
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_7
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_8
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_9
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_10
			}
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_encouraged_education_1
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_1
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_2
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_3
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_4
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_4
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_5
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_5
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_6
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_6
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_6
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_7
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_7
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_7
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_8
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_8
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_8
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_9
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_9
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_9
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_10

TUR_import_dependence_level_up = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_5 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_5
			add_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_6
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_4 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_4
			add_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_3 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_3
			add_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_2
			add_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons
			add_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { 
			NOT = { has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons }
			NOT = { has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_2 }
			NOT = { has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_3 }
			NOT = { has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_4 }
			NOT = { has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_5 }
			NOT = { has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_6 }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_domestic_weapon_companies }
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons
	}
}

TUR_yildiz_teskilati_factions_variable_round_value = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power
					value = 1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power
					value = 0
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power
					value = 1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power
					value = 0
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power = 0 }
		}
	}
}

TUR_modernize_navy_effect = {
	effect_tooltip = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_army_of_bygone_era_just_navy
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_army_of_bygone_era_just_navy
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_army_of_bygone_era
				add_idea = TUR_army_of_bygone_era_no_navy
			}
		}
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TUR_army_of_bygone_era }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_army_of_bygone_era
				add_idea = TUR_army_of_bygone_era_no_navy
			}

TUR_legitimacy_level_up = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_terrible }
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_terrible
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_high }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_high
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal
		}
	}
}
TUR_legitimacy_level_down = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_high }
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_high
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_terrible }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_terrible
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low
		}
	}
}

ottoman_minority_variable_check_konstantiniyye = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			347 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_southslav_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_kurd_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_assyrian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_turkish_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_region scope = TUR }
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_konstantiniyye = 1 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			347 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_konstantiniyye = 2 }
		}
	}

			347 = {

			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {

	}

			}
		}
		every_country = {

		}
	}
	if = {

			}
		}
		every_country = {

		}
	}
	if = {

		limit = {
			107 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_southslav_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_kurd_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_assyrian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_turkish_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_region scope = TUR }
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_serbia = 1 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			107 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_serbia = 2 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			107 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_serbia = 3 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			107 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_serbia = 4 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			107 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_southslav_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_serbia = 5 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			107 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_serbia = 6 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			107 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_kurd_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_serbia = 7 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			107 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_serbia = 8 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			107 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {

	if = {

				is_controlled_by = ROOT

			}
		}
		every_country = {

		}
	}
}

TUR_lower_party_factionalism = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_character = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism
			}
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism
			}
			swap_country_leader_traits = {
				remove = TUR_inner_party_factionalism
				add = TUR_inner_party_factionalism2
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_character = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism2
			}
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism2
			}
			swap_country_leader_traits = {
				remove = TUR_inner_party_factionalism2
				add = TUR_inner_party_factionalism3
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_character = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism3
			}
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism3
			}
			remove_country_leader_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism3
		}
	}
}
TUR_remove_party_factionalism = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_character = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism
			}
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism
			}
			remove_country_leader_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_character = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism2
			}
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism2
			}
			remove_country_leader_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_character = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism3
			}
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism3
			}
			remove_country_leader_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism3
		}
	}
}
TUR_add_party_factionalism = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_character = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism
			}
		}
		add_country_leader_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_character = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism2
			}
		}
		add_country_leader_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism2
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_character = {
				has_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism3
			}
		}
		add_country_leader_trait = TUR_inner_party_factionalism3
	}
}

TUR_add_supported_local_designers_land = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = TUR_supported_local_designers_sea
				has_idea = TUR_supported_local_designers_air
			}
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_supported_local_designers_land
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_supported_local_designers_sea
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_supported_local_designers_land_sea
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_supported_local_designers_air
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_supported_local_designers_land_air
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_supported_local_designers_sea
			has_idea = TUR_supported_local_designers_air
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_supported_local_designers_land_sea_air
	}
}

TUR_remove_debt_0295 = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = opda_lira
			check_variable = { opda_lira > 0.294 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_0295
		add_to_variable = {
			opda_lira = -0.295
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			opda_consumer_goods = -0.01
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			opda_resources_to_market = -0.005
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = opda_lira
			check_variable = { opda_lira < 0.295 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_existing_amount
		multiply_variable = {
			opda_lira = 0
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			opda_consumer_goods = 0
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			opda_resources_to_market = 0
		}
	}
}

TUR_increase_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = {
	add_to_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty > 3 }
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = 3 }
	}
	effect_tooltip = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_minimal_power_disloyal
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_minimal_power_disloyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_minimal_power_neutral
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_decreased_power_disloyal
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_decreased_power_disloyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_decreased_power_neutral
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_limited_power_disloyal
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_limited_power_disloyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_limited_power_neutral
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_extended_power_disloyal
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_extended_power_disloyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_extended_power_neutral
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_disloyal
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_disloyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_neutral
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_minimal_power_neutral
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_minimal_power_neutral
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_minimal_power_loyal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_decreased_power_neutral
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_decreased_power_neutral
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_decreased_power_loyal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_limited_power_neutral
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_limited_power_neutral
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_limited_power_loyal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_extended_power_neutral
			}

				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_extended_power_neutral

}

		}
		else_if = {

				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_decreased_power_disloyal

			}
		}
		if = {

			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_minimal_power_disloyal

				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_extended_power_disloyal
			}
		}
		if = {

TUR_calculate_harbiyeli_officer_values = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_loyal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = 3 }
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_power = 4 }
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_loyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_extended_power_loyal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = 3 }
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_power = 3 }
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_loyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_limited_power_loyal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = 3 }
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_power = 2 }
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_loyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_decreased_power_loyal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = 3 }
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_power = 1 }
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_loyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_minimal_power_loyal
			}
		}
		###
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = 2 }
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_power = 5 }
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_loyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_neutral
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = 2 }
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_power = 4 }
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_loyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_extended_power_neutral
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = 2 }
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_power = 3 }
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_loyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_limited_power_neutral
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = 2 }
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_power = 2 }
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_powerful_loyal
				add_idea = TUR_harbiyeli_officers_decreased_power_neutral
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = 2 }
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_power = 1 }
